)@@G@@        PUT               . NO, PUT OUT IMAGE   @G@@@@          LA      NW
)@@G@@  A0,LC             . CALACULATE OLDEST CYCLE NUMBER  @D@@@@          AANX
)@@G@@,U      A0,1              . (OC=LC+1-CC)  @B@@@@          AN        A0,CNY

)@@G@@@E@@@@/         . ROUTINE TO HANDLE 'FILE' AND 'LOAD' COMMANDS.   @F@@@@PK
)@@G@@          . MUST FILE OUTPUT AND RESET FILENAMES SO THAT INPUT    @G@@@@PL
)@@G@@          . IS READ FROM OUTPUT FILE. CYCLE INCREMENTING IS PERMITTED.  PM
)@@G@@@]@@@@          . @]@@@@DFIL1*    . @F@@@@          SZ        LODC      PN
)@@G@@        . CLEAR 'LOAD' CMND FLAG.   @A@@@@DFIL11    . ENTRY FROM LOAD CMPO
)@@G@@ND.   @D@@@@          L,U       A0,1              . GET FLAG.     @D@@@@PP
)@@G@@          TZ        INISOUT           . IS IN ELT=OUT.@D@@@@          SZPQ
)@@G@@        A0                . YES, CLEAR.   @E@@@@          S         A0,NPR
)@@G@@EWFIL         . SET NAME IS NEW.    @E@@@@          DL        A0,OUTBL+2PS
)@@G@@        . GET CURRENT ELTN.   @C@@@@          DS        A0,ELTSV        PT
)@@G@@  . SAVE IT.@C@@@@          DL        A0,OUTBL+6        . VERSION.@C@@@@PU
)@@G@@          DS        A0,VERSV          . SAVE IT.@E@@@@          L       PV
)@@G@@  A0,DOPTO          . GET OUTPUT OPTION.  @C@@@@          S         A0,DPW
)@@G@@OPTOS         . SAVE IT.@D@@@@          L         A1,EDCT           . GEPX
)@@G@@T CURR POS. @G@@@@          TG        A1,COUNT          . IS THRE MORE OPY
)@@G@@N INPT IMAGE.     @C@@@@          J         DFIL4             . NO.     PZ
)@@G@@@D@@@@          DL        A2,ASCBL          . GET BLANKS.   @G@@@@      QA

)@@G@@2 .  INITIALIZE VIRTUAL ORIGIN SUM  @F@@@@         LOAD  A13,1,I .     SSE
)@@G@@ET CONSTANT FOR EXTENT CALCULATIONS @C@@@@ . ** FORM MULTIPLIERS AND VIRSF
)@@G@@TUAL ORIGIN **    @F@@@@EXALL7   LABEL .             TOP OF LOOP, COMPUTSG
)@@G@@E VIRUAL ORIGIN   @G@@@@         STORE A4,W1,X3 .    SET MULTIPLIER INTOSH

)@@G@@BOUND (L(I))@C@@@@         MPYS  A8,A4 .       A8 = M(I) * L(I)   @H@@@@SJ
)@@G@@         SUB   A7,A8 .       FORM VIRTUAL ORIGIN = SUM(-M(I)*L(I))+REAL SK
)@@G@@ORIGIN@E@@@@EXALL8   LABEL .             COMPUTE AND TEST MULTIPLIER    SL
)@@G@@@F@@@@         AU,H1 A13,1,*X3 .   A14 = EXTENT(I)               *******SM
)@@G@@@F@@@@         MPYS  A4,A14 .      COMPUTE MULTIPLIER M(I) * EXTENT (I) SN
)@@G@@@F@@@@         IF    A4,GE,KEXTNT,I THEN,EXMPOV . -> MULTIPLIER OVERFLOWSO
)@@G@@@G@@@@         TLEM,XU X1,0,X3 .   I := I - 1, M(I) := M(I+1) * EXTENT(ISP
)@@G@@+1)   @C@@@@         GOTO  EXALL7 .      -> MORE DIMENSIONS @F@@@@ . ** SQ
)@@G@@SET VIRTUAL ORIGIN IN DOPE VECTOR AND INITIALIZE ARRAY **   @F@@@@      SR
)@@G@@   STORE A7,ARDVOR,X1 .          IMPLANT VIRTUAL ORIGIN     @I@@@@      SS
)@@G@@   IF    SDARST*01000,OFF THEN,EXALL9 . -> FINISH NON-STRING ARRAY INITIST
)@@G@@AL    @C@@@@ . ** ALLOCATE SECONDARY STRING DOPE VECTORS ** @H@@@@      SU
)@@G@@   ADD   A4,W1XU,X2 .  FIRST FREE WORD BEYOND SECONDARY DOPE VECTORS    SV
)@@G@@@D@@@@EXALS3   LABEL .                   TRY TO FIND STORAGE@G@@@@      SW
)@@G@@   IF    A4,LT,ADPCND THEN,EXALS2 . -> STORAGE CAPACITY EXCEEDED? @D@@@@SX
)@@G@@         LOCAL .                   SAVE RETURN ADDRESS@D@@@@         LINSY
)@@G@@K    WROVFL .          GET MORE STORAGE   @G@@@@         UNSTK   X11 .  SZ
)@@G@@           RECLAIM RETURN ADDRESS FROM STACK    @E@@@@         GOTO    ETA
)@@G@@XALS3 .          GO BACK AND TRY AGAIN    @E@@@@EXALS2   LABEL .        TB
)@@G@@           HERE WITH ENOUGH STORAGE @H@@@@         AU    A9,A4 .       ATC
)@@G@@10 = FIRST WORD OF 1ST SECONDARY DOPE VECTOR    @F@@@@EXALS1   LABEL .  TD
)@@G@@           INITIALIZE A SECONDARY DOPE VECTOR   @F@@@@         STORE A10TE
)@@G@@,ARDVOR,X2 .         SET FLAGS AND WORD POINTER @F@@@@         STORE A11TF

)@@G@@ HAS LAST SECONDARY DOPE VECTOR BEEN COMPLETED? @F@@@@         GOTO  EXATI
)@@G@@LS1 .      NO, -> INITIALIZE NEXT DOPE VECTOR   @E@@@@ . ** COMPUTE END TJ

)@@G@@     REMOVE FLAG AND CLASS INFORMATION    @F@@@@         STORE A10,A2 . TL
)@@G@@     A2 - A(FIRST FREE WORD AFTER STRINGS)@F@@@@         SUB   A10,W1XU,TM
)@@G@@X2 . A10 = NUMBER OF WORDS TO INITIALIZE  @C@@@@         LOAD  R1,A10 . TN
)@@G@@     SET NUMBER FOR BT  @G@@@@         GOTO  EXCLR1 .      INITIALIZE STTO
)@@G@@RINGS (USING A3) AND RETURN   @C@@@@EXMPOV*  LABEL .             MULTIPLTP
)@@G@@IER OVERFLOW@^@@@@         ONER EREXMP,3 .@F@@@@ . ' MULTIPLIER OVERFLOWTQ
)@@G@@ DURING INITIALIZATION OF ARRAY', SDX4.   @I@@@@/ . --------------------TR
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------    @E@@@@ . ***TS
)@@G@@ EXECUTION CONTROL:  ARRAY EXPRESSION BOUNDS CHECKER  @I@@@@ . ---------TT
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------------    TU
)@@G@@@F@@@@ . CALLED BY COMPILED CODE TO DO SUBSCRIPTING IN ARRAY EXPRESSION TV
)@@G@@@]@@@@ . INPUT:   @D@@@@ .       A1  = ADDRESS OF LIST OF FULL WORD SUBSTW
)@@G@@CRIPTS@C@@@@ .       A2  = ADDRESS OF ARRAY'S DOPE VECTOR   @E@@@@ .    TX
)@@G@@   X11 --->       SF        SELECTOR BITS WORD (SBW)  @E@@@@ .          TY
)@@G@@                 SH        SD POINTER FOR ARRAY @F@@@@ .                TZ
)@@G@@           SH        DIMENSIONALITY OF ARRAY    @C@@@@ .                UA
)@@G@@           (RETURN TO HERE)   @H@@@@ .       THIS ROUTINE IS CALLED INDIUB
)@@G@@RECTLY THROUGH THE ADDRESS STORED AS THE  @G@@@@ . FIRST WORD IN THE TALUC
)@@G@@LY CELL VECTOR (TCV).  USING THE U-FIELD OF THE @H@@@@ . LMJ WHICH CALLSUD
)@@G@@ THIS ROUTINE, THE ADDRESS OF THE TCV CAN BE CALCULATED.    @H@@@@ . AFTUE
)@@G@@ER THE FIRST TIME THROUGH EVALUATING THE ARRAY EXPRESSION, SUBSCRIPT    UF
)@@G@@@H@@@@ . CHECKING IS DISABLED BY CHANGING THE ADDRESS IN THE 1ST WORD OFUG
)@@G@@ THE TCV.   @F@@@@ . THE NEXT PART OF THE TCV CONTAINS A LIST OF BOUNDS UH
)@@G@@EXPRESSIONS @G@@@@ . (EXTENT - 1,LOWER BOUND) FOR THE REPRESENTATIVE AGGUI
)@@G@@REGATE EXPRESSION.@G@@@@ . THE REST OF THE TCV IS A LIST OF OFFSETS OF TUJ
)@@G@@HE SUBSCRIPTS FROM THE  @F@@@@ . LOWER BOUND, GIVING THE STATUS OF WHICHUK
)@@G@@ ELEMENT OF THE ARRAY   @A@@@@ . EXPRESSION IS BEING EVALUATED.   @]@@@@UL
)@@G@@ . ACTION:  @G@@@@ .       IF THE N-TH BIT OF THE SELECTOR BITS WORD (SBUM
)@@G@@W) IS SET THEN THE@D@@@@ . BOUNDS OF THE (N+1)TH SUBSCRIPT IN THE DOPE VUN
)@@G@@ECTOR @G@@@@ . ARE COMPARED FOR EQUALITY WITH THE APPROPRIATE BOUNDS EXPUO
)@@G@@RESSION     @F@@@@ . IN THE TCV.  IF THEY ARE NOT EQUAL, AN IMCOMPATIBLIUP
)@@G@@TY MESSAGE  @G@@@@ . IS SENT, HOWEVER, IF THE EXTENTS ARE NOT EQUAL, A TUQ
)@@G@@ERMINAL ERROR     @#@@@@ . IS SIGNALLED.  @]@@@@ . RETURN:  @B@@@@ .    UR
)@@G@@   A1  = ADDRESS OF DESIRED ELEMENT @ @@@@ . INTERNAL REGISTER USAGE:   US
)@@G@@@E@@@@ .       X1  (A1) . -> LIST OF SUBSCRIPTS (1 IN INCREMENTOR)@D@@@@UT
)@@G@@ .       X2  (A2) . -> ORIGINAL DV (2 IN INCREMENTOR) @B@@@@ .       X3 UU
)@@G@@ = POINTER TO SD OF ARRAY     @D@@@@ .       X4      = LAST ADDRESS OF SUV
)@@G@@UBSCRIPT LIST     @ @@@@ .       X5 = POINTER TO TCV  @^@@@@ .       A1 UW
)@@G@@ = SCRATCH  @B@@@@ .       A4  = SELECTOR BITS WORD (SBW)   @B@@@@EXTLYCUX
)@@G@@*  LLOC . ENTRY POINT FROM USER CODE@C@@@@         LMJ   X5,EXSAVE .   SUY
)@@G@@AVE REGISTERS     @F@@@@         LOAD  X11,W1XU+1,X11 .        RETURN POUZ
)@@G@@INT SKIPS SBW     @I@@@@         LOCAL .                       SAVE RETUVA
)@@G@@RN POINT AFTER SUBSCRIPT COMPUTA    @D@@@@         SUB   X11,2,I .     PVB
)@@G@@OINT TO CALLER'S LMJ    @D@@@@         LOADXI A1,1,I .     SET SUBSCRIPTVC
)@@G@@ INCREMENTOR@E@@@@         LOADXI A2,2,I .     SET DOPE VECTOR INCREMENTVD
)@@G@@OR    @F@@@@         LOAD  X3,W1H1+2,X11 .         POINTER TO SD OF ARRAVE
)@@G@@Y     @F@@@@         LOAD  X4,W1XH2+2,X11 .        DIMENSIONALITY OF ARRVF
)@@G@@AY - 1@F@@@@         ADD     X4,A1 .           POINT TO END OF SUBSCRIPTVG
)@@G@@ LIST @A@@@@         LOAD  A6,W1+1,X11 . SBW    @F@@@@         STORED A1VH
)@@G@@,X1 .      COPY SUBSCRIPTLIST AND DV POINTER    @E@@@@         LOAD  X5,VI
)@@G@@W1H2,X11 . ADDRESS FIELD OF LMJ = A (TCV) @F@@@@         SUB   X5,020000VJ
)@@G@@0,I .          REMOVE INCREMENTOR (I) BIT @E@@@@         ADD     X5,W1U,VK
)@@G@@X10 .      ADD IN ADDRESS OF AREC   @D@@@@         LOADXI X5,1,I .     SVL
)@@G@@ET INCREMENTOR OF TCV   @E@@@@EXTLY1   LABEL .             TOP OF LOOP TVM
)@@G@@O CHECK BOUNDS    @E@@@@         JNS   A6,EXTLY3 .   -> BIT ON, NON-STARVN
)@@G@@ SUBSCRIPT  @F@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1+1,*X5 . EXTENT-1,LOWER BOUND FROMVO
)@@G@@ TALLY CELL @D@@@@         USING WORD,X2 .     X2 = A(MPLR, BOUNDS) - 2 VP
)@@G@@@E@@@@         IF    A4,EQ,W1+3 THEN,EXTLY4 . -> BOUNDS MATCH     @C@@@@VQ
)@@G@@         LOAD  A4,W1H1,X5 .  EXTENT-1 FROM TCV  @G@@@@         IF    A4,VR
)@@G@@EQ,W1H1+3 THEN,EXTLY5 . -> AT LEAST EXTENTS MATCH     @E@@@@         ONEVS
)@@G@@R EREXTLY1,3 . EXTENT MISMATCH, TERMINAL ERROR  @H@@@@ . 'EXTENT OF ',SDVT
)@@G@@X3, 'DOES NOT MATCH EXTENTS IN THE REST OF THE EXPRESSION.' @F@@@@EXTLY5VU
)@@G@@   LABEL .             EXTENTS MATCH, LOWER BOUNDS DO NOT   @F@@@@      VV
)@@G@@   USING SDSECT,X3 .   SEE IF WARNING GIVEN FOR THIS ARRAY  @H@@@@      VW
)@@G@@   IF    SD5MG2,ON,SDCLS5 THEN,EXTLY4 . -> WARNING MESSAGE ALREADY GIVENVX
)@@G@@@B@@@@         ONER EREXTLY2,0 . BOUNDS MISMATCH@E@@@@ . 'PL1/F INCOMPATVY
)@@G@@IBILITY.  BOUNDS OF ',SDX3, 'DO NOT MATCH @B@@@@ . BOUNDS IN THE REST OFVZ
)@@G@@ THE EXPRESSION   @H@@@@         SET   SD5MG2,ON,SDCLS5 .      SET FLAG WA
)@@G@@TO INHIBIT FURTHER WARNINGS   @F@@@@EXTLY4   LABEL .             SEE IF WB
)@@G@@AT START OF SUBSCRIPT LIST    @F@@@@         USING WORD,X1 .     IS THISWC
)@@G@@ FIRST TIME BOUNDS CHECKED?   @G@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1H2+3,X2 .       WD
)@@G@@   LOWER BOUND FROM DOPE VECTOR     @G@@@@         IF    A4,NE,W1H2 THENWE
)@@G@@,EXTLY7 . -> SECOND TIME THROUGH ARRAY    @E@@@@EXTLY3   LABEL .        WF
)@@G@@     BUMP TO NEXT POSITION IN LISTS @E@@@@         ADD   X2,2,I .      -WG
)@@G@@> NEXT POSITION IN DV - 2     @H@@@@         TLEM,XU X1,0,X4 .   INCREMEWH
)@@G@@NT SUBSCRIPT LIST, CHECK IF END REACHED   @E@@@@         GOTO  EXTLY1 . WI
)@@G@@     NO, ->CHECK NEXT DIMENSION     @F@@@@         GOTO  EXSUB1 .      YWJ
)@@G@@ES, -> COMPUTE SUBSCRIPT ADDRESS    @F@@@@EXTLY7   LABEL .             SWK
)@@G@@ECOND TIME THROUGH ARRAY EXPRESSION @F@@@@         UNSTK X11 .         FWL
)@@G@@ETCH CALLERS ADDRESS FROM PIT STACK @F@@@@         STACK X11 .         IWM
)@@G@@N CASE IT WAS DESTROYED BY ONER     @C@@@@         SUB   X11,2,I .     PWN
)@@G@@OINT TO TCV HEAD  @G@@@@         LOADA A4,EXSUB2 .   CHANGE TCV TO ELIMIWO
)@@G@@NATE BOUNDS CHECKING    @D@@@@         LOAD    X11,W1H2,X11 .    GET OFFWP
)@@G@@SET OF TCV  @E@@@@         SUB     X11,0200000,I .   TAKE OUT INDIRECT BWQ
)@@G@@IT    @D@@@@         LOAD    X11,W1U,X10 .     ADD IN AREC OFFSET @D@@@@WR
)@@G@@         STORE A4,W1,X11 .   STORE NEW ADDRESS IN TCV @D@@@@         GOTWS
)@@G@@O  EXSUB1 .      -> COMPUTE SUBSCRIPTS    @H@@@@EXSUB2   LABEL .        WT
)@@G@@     ENTRY POINT AFTER SUBSCRIPT CHECKING TURNED OFF  @B@@@@         ADDWU
)@@G@@   X11,1,I .     SKIP SBW     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@.         THIS CODE IS MWV
)@@G@@AGIC - - - CONTINUE TO NEXTXPAGE    @[@@@@.     @I@@@@/ . --------------WW
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------    @C@@@@WX
)@@G@@ . ***EXECUTION CONTROL:  SUBSCRIPT COMPUTER ***@I@@@@ . ---------------WY
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------    @C@@@@WZ
)@@G@@ . CALLED BY COMPILED CODE TO DO SUBSCRIPTING   @C@@@@ . A1  = ADDRESS OXA
)@@G@@F LIST OF FULL WORD SUBSCRIPTS@B@@@@ . A2  = ADDRESS OF ARRAY'S DOPE VECXB
)@@G@@TOR   @D@@@@ . X11  --->            SH        SD POINTER FOR ARRAY@F@@@@XC
)@@G@@ .                           SH        DIMENSIONALITY OF ARRAY - 1@C@@@@XD
)@@G@@ .                           (RETURN POINT)     @]@@@@ . ACTION:  @G@@@@XE
)@@G@@ .       THE ADDRESS OF THE ARRAY ELEMENT SPECIFIED BY THE SUBSCRIPT    XF
)@@G@@@F@@@@ . VALUES AND THE CONTENTS OF THE DOPE VECTOR ARE USED TO COMPUTE XG
)@@G@@@D@@@@ . THE REAL ADDRESS OF THE SPECIFIED ARRAY ELEMENT.   @]@@@@ . RETXH
)@@G@@URN:  @B@@@@ .       A1  = ADDRESS OF DESIRED ELEMENT @ @@@@ . INTERNAL XI
)@@G@@REGISTER USAGE:   @B@@@@ .       X1  (A1)       = A(SUBSCRIPTS)   @B@@@@XJ
)@@G@@ .       X2  (A2)       = A(DOPE VECTOR)  @D@@@@ .       X3             XK
)@@G@@     = SD POINTER FOR ARRAY   @F@@@@ .       X4                  = HIGHEXL
)@@G@@ST ADDRESS IN SUBSCRIPT LIST  @F@@@@ .       X5                  = RETURXM
)@@G@@N ADDRESS FOR REGISTER SAVE   @F@@@@ .       X11                 = RETURXN
)@@G@@N ADDRESS (SAVED ON PIT STACK)@C@@@@ .       A1 TO A2            = WORK XO
)@@G@@REGISTERS   @C@@@@EXSUB*   LOCAL .             SAVE ENTRY POINT   @C@@@@XP
)@@G@@         LMJ   X5,EXSAVE .   SAVE REGISTERS USED@E@@@@         LOADXI A1XQ
)@@G@@,1,I .     SET SUBSCRIPT LIST INCREMENTOR @E@@@@         LOADXI A2,2,I .XR
)@@G@@     SET DOPE VECTOR INCREMENTOR    @E@@@@         LOAD  X4,W1XH2,X11 . XS
)@@G@@         DIMENSIONALITY - 1   @E@@@@         ADD   X4,A1 .       TOP ADDXT
)@@G@@RESS OF SUBSCRIPT LIST  @D@@@@         LOAD  X3,W1H1,X11 . SD POINTER FOXU
)@@G@@R ARRAY     @E@@@@EXSUB1   LABEL .             ENTRY FROM TCV BOUNDS CHEXV
)@@G@@CKING @G@@@@         STORED A1,X1              . CLEAR A1,A2 FOR OTHER PXW
)@@G@@URPOSES     @F@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1S1,X2 .  CHECK FLAG FOR UNALLOCATEXX
)@@G@@D ARRAY     @^@@@@         AND,U A3,1 .   @ @@@@         JNZ   A4,EXSUBUXY
)@@G@@ .    @G@@@@         LOAD  A1,W1,*X2 .   GET VIRTUAL ORIGIN AND ADVANCE XZ
)@@G@@DV POINTER  @B@@@@EXSUB3   LABEL .             TOP OF LOOP  @D@@@@      YA
)@@G@@   LOAD  A5,W1,X1 .    PICK UP I-TH SUBSCRIPT   @D@@@@         LOAD  A3,YB
)@@G@@W1+1,X2 .  EXTENT(I)-1, LOWER BOUND @F@@@@         TLE,XU A5,0,*A3 .   CYC
)@@G@@HECK SUBSCRIPT AGAINST LOWER BOUND  @D@@@@         GOTO  EXSUBL .      -YD
)@@G@@> SUBSCRIPT TOO LOW     @D@@@@         TG,XU  A5,0,A3            . CHECKYE
)@@G@@ HIGH BOUND @G@@@@         TNE,XU  A5,0,A3       . A5>A3 THEN INDEX OUT YF
)@@G@@OF BOUNDS-->FIX UP@D@@@@         GOTO  EXSUB4              . COMPUTE SUBYG
)@@G@@SCRIPT@D@@@@EXSUBH   LABEL .                   SUBSCRIPT TOO LARGE@D@@@@YH
)@@G@@         LA,XU  A5,0,A3            . USE UPPER BOUND  @D@@@@EXSUBE   LABYI
)@@G@@EL .             MERGE FOR ERROR MESSAGE  @F@@@@         ONUNIT  EREXSUBYJ
)@@G@@1,ACCDSU,2  R,I,R  DEXWK1,4  DEXMAX,4     @B@@@@ . 'SUBSCRIPT IS OUT OF YK
)@@G@@BOUNDS IN ', SDX3.@F@@@@EXSUB4   LABEL .             MERGE WHEN SUBSCRIPYL
)@@G@@T IS WITHIN RANGE @G@@@@         MPYS  A5,W1,*X2 .   A5 = MPLR(I) * SUBSYM
)@@G@@CRIPT(I), I := I + 1    @D@@@@         ADD   A1,A5 .       COMPUTE REAL YN
)@@G@@ADDRESS SUM @G@@@@         TLEM,XU  X1,0,X4          . CHECK FOR END OF YO
)@@G@@SS LIST,ADV PTR   @C@@@@         GOTO  EXSUB3 .      ->MORE SUBSCRIPTS  YP
)@@G@@@C@@@@         LINK  EXUNSV .      RESTORE REGISTERS  @E@@@@         JMPYQ
)@@G@@   1 .           -> RETURN TO USER CODE CALLER  @C@@@@EXSUBL   LABEL .  YR
)@@G@@           SUBSCRIPT TOO LOW  @G@@@@         LOAD  A5,W1XH2+1,X2 .      YS
)@@G@@   USE SIGN EXTENDED LOWER BOUND    @E@@@@         GOTO  EXSUBE .      MYT
)@@G@@ERGE WITH ERROR PROCESSING    @E@@@@EXSUBU   LABEL .             UNINITIYU
)@@G@@ALIZED ARRAY REFERENCED @ @@@@         ONER EREXUD02,3 .    @A@@@@ . SDXYV
)@@G@@3, ' HAS NOT BEEN ALLOCATED.' @I@@@@/ . --------------------------------YW
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------    @E@@@@ . *** EXECUTION CYX
)@@G@@ONTROL:  AGGREGATE TEMPORARY ALLOCATOR    @I@@@@ . ---------------------YY
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------    @E@@@@ . CALYZ
)@@G@@LED BY COMPILED CODE TO ALLOCATE STORAGE FOR TEMPORARY@B@@@@ . ARGUMENT ZA
)@@G@@TO A USER DEFINED FUNCTION.   @]@@@@ . INPUT:   @G@@@@ .       A1       ZB
)@@G@@      = ADDRESS OF PARMS DV TEMPLATE IF ARGUMENT IS   @B@@@@ .          ZC
)@@G@@                   A CONSTANT @H@@@@ .                           = ADDREZD
)@@G@@SS OF DV OF REPRESENTATIVE DATA ITEM IN   @D@@@@ .                      ZE
)@@G@@       ARGUMENT EXPRESSION    @D@@@@ .       A2             = ADDRESS OFZF
)@@G@@ STRING LENGTHS   @E@@@@ .       X11  --->      SF        SELECTOR BITS ZG
)@@G@@WORD (SBW)  @E@@@@ .                           SH        PARAMETER SD POZH
)@@G@@INTER @E@@@@ .                           SH        PARAMETER DV LENGTH  ZI
)@@G@@@C@@@@ .                           (RETURN TO HERE)   @]@@@@ . RETURN:  ZJ
)@@G@@@F@@@@ .       A1             = ADDRESS OF NEW DOPE VECTOR FOR ARGUMENT ZK
)@@G@@@]@@@@ . ACTION:  @E@@@@ .       SPACE IS ALLOCATED FOR AN AGGREGATE DOPZL
)@@G@@E VECTOR    @F@@@@ .       THE DOPE VECTOR IS INITIALIZED USING BOUNDS FZM
)@@G@@ROM THE     @F@@@@ . SUPPLIED DOPE VECTOR.  THE SELECTOR BITS ARE USED TZN
)@@G@@O DECIDE    @A@@@@ . WHICH BOUNDS ARE TO BE USED.     @G@@@@ .       EXAZO
)@@G@@LL0 IS USED TO COMPLETE THE ALLOCATION FOR THE ARGUMENT.    @ @@@@ . INTZP
)@@G@@ERNAL REGISTER USAGE:   @C@@@@ .       X9              = OLD AREPTR, A(NZQ
)@@G@@EW DV)@C@@@@ .       A3-A4               = SCRATCH FOR IF'S @E@@@@ .    ZR
)@@G@@   X8             = LIST OF MAXIMUM STRING LENGTHS    @D@@@@ .       X1 ZS
)@@G@@             = POINTER TO NEW DOPE VECTOR @E@@@@ .       X6             ZT
)@@G@@= A(REPRESENTATIVE DATA ITEM DV)    @C@@@@ .       A7              = SELZU
)@@G@@ECTOR BITS WORD   @C@@@@ .       A5              =SCRATCH FOR LENGTHS   ZV
)@@G@@@D@@@@ .       X7             =SAVE ADDRESS OF DV FOR RETURN@E@@@@ .    ZW
)@@G@@   A1              =SCRATCH FOR TOP OF STACK CHECKING @A@@@@ .       A6 ZX
)@@G@@   = SCRATCH FOR MOVES  @F@@@@ .       A15 [DEXWK1]        = SD POINTER ZY
)@@G@@OF ORIGINAL ARGUMENT    @E@@@@ .       X4              = SD POINTER TO CZZ
)@@G@@URRENT ELEMENT    @D@@@@EXTMP1*  LLOC .              ENTRY FROM USER CODAA
)@@G@@E     @F@@@@         LMJ   X5,EXMST .    SAVE REGISTERS IN ACTIVATION REAB
)@@G@@CORD  @C@@@@         LOADXM X9,AREPTR,X10 .        A(NEW DV)@G@@@@      AC
)@@G@@   LOADXM X7,AREPTR,X10 .        SAVE ADDRESS FOR RETURN LATER    @C@@@@AD
)@@G@@         LOADXM X8,A2 .      A(LIST OF LENGTHS) @E@@@@         LOAD  X6,AE
)@@G@@A1 .       A(REPRESENTATIVE DATA ITEM DV) @F@@@@         LOAD  A1,W1H2+1AF
)@@G@@,X11 .         NEW DOPE VECTOR LENGTH     @D@@@@         ADD   A1,W1XU,XAG
)@@G@@9 .  X1  = NEW TOP OF STACK   @F@@@@         STORE A1,AREPTR,X10 .      AH
)@@G@@   UPDATE ACTIVATION RECORD   @E@@@@EXTMP2   LABEL .                   HAI
)@@G@@ERE TO LOOK FOR STORAGE @G@@@@         IF    A1,LT,ADPCND THEN,EXTMP3 . AJ
)@@G@@->STORAGE CAPACITY EXCEEDED?  @D@@@@         LOCAL .                   SAK
)@@G@@AVE RETURN ADDRESS@D@@@@         LINK    WROVFL .          GET MORE STORAL
)@@G@@AGE   @E@@@@         UNSTK   X11 .             RECLAIM RETURN ADDRESS   AM
)@@G@@@D@@@@         GOTO    EXTMP2 .          TRY TO FIT AGAIN   @D@@@@EXTMP3AN
)@@G@@   LABEL .                   GOT ENOUGH ROOM NOW@C@@@@         LOAD  A6,AO
)@@G@@W1,X11 .   SELECTOR BITS WORD @B@@@@         STORE A6,DEXWK2 .   SAVE SBAP
)@@G@@W     @F@@@@         LSDP  X4,W1H1+1,X11 . X4  = SD POINTER OF 'ARGUMENTAQ
)@@G@@'     @D@@@@         LOAD  A15,W1XU,X4 . SAVE FOR LATER COMPARISON@E@@@@AR
)@@G@@ . ** FOLLOW POINTERS THROUGH STRUCTURE TO BASE ELEMENTS    @D@@@@EXTP11AS
)@@G@@   LABEL .             LOOK FOR BASE ELEMENT    @ @@@@         USING   SAT
)@@G@@DSECT,X4 .  @G@@@@         IF    SDSTRU,OFF,SDCLS4 THEN,EXTP12 . -> BASEAU
)@@G@@ ELEMENT FOUND    @D@@@@         LSDP  X4,SDSON,X4 . FOLLOW POINTER TO SAV
)@@G@@ON    @D@@@@         GOTO  EXTP11 .      -> TEST SON FOR SON, ETC @D@@@@AW
)@@G@@ . ** ASSEMBLE DOPE VECTOR FOR TEMPORARY ARGUMENT **  @#@@@@EXTP12   LABAX
)@@G@@EL .  @D@@@@         LOAD  X1,W1XU,X9 .  BASE OF NEW DOPE VECTOR  @C@@@@AY
)@@G@@         LOAD  A7,DEXWK2 .   SELECTOR BITS WORD @F@@@@         IF    SDAAZ
)@@G@@RST,OFF,SDCLS1 THEN,EXT111 . -> NON-STRINGS     @E@@@@         LOAD  A5,BA
)@@G@@W1,*X8 .   LENGTH OF TEMP STRING NEEDED   @D@@@@         TN    A5 .     BB
)@@G@@     NEGATIVE STRING LENGTH   @E@@@@         TG,U  A5,MXSTLN+1 . STRING BC
)@@G@@LENGTH WITHIN BOUNDS?   @D@@@@         LINK  EXTMSL .      IMPROPER STRIBD
)@@G@@NG LENGTH   @G@@@@         STORE A5,W1H1+1,X1 .          SET MAXIMUM STRBE
)@@G@@ING LENGTH FIELD  @G@@@@         STORE A5,W1H2+1,X1 .          SET CURREBF
)@@G@@NT STRING LENGTH FIELD  @D@@@@EXT111   LABEL .             MERGE FOR NONBG
)@@G@@-STRINGS    @G@@@@         IF    SDARRY,ON,SDCLS2 THEN,EXTP08 . -> PARAMBH
)@@G@@ETER IS ARRAY     @G@@@@         IF    SDARST,ON,SDCLS1 THEN,EXTP09 . ->BI
)@@G@@ SCALER STRING PARAMETER@E@@@@         ADD   X9,1,I .      SCALER, NON-SBJ
)@@G@@TRING, FULLWORD DV@[@@@@.     @D@@@@.        MIGHT THIS SUPPOSED TO BE JBK
)@@G@@NS?   PRM 5/22/75 @[@@@@.     @E@@@@         JNZ   A7,EXTP04 .   -> ARGUBL
)@@G@@MENT CAME FROM ARRAY    @E@@@@         ADD   X6,1,I .      SCALER, NON-SBM
)@@G@@TRING ARGUMENT    @F@@@@         GOTO  EXTP10 .      -> ALLOCATE SPACE FBN
)@@G@@OR DUMMY ARGUMENT @#@@@@EXTP08   LABEL .  @G@@@@         LOAD  A5,SDNDIMBO
)@@G@@,X4 .          NUMBER OF DIMENSIONS IN PARAMETER@F@@@@ . ** MOVE SELECTEBP
)@@G@@D BOUNDS PAIRS FROM ARGUMENT DOPE VECTOR TO     @ @@@@ .    TEMPORARY DOBQ
)@@G@@PE VECTOR **@#@@@@EXTP05   LABEL .  @F@@@@         ADD   X9,2,I .      BBR
)@@G@@UMP POINTER TO NEXT SLOT IN TEMP DV @#@@@@EXTP03   LABEL .  @G@@@@      BS
)@@G@@   ADD   X6,2,I .      BUMP POINTER TO NEXT SLOT IN ARGUMENT DV   @F@@@@BT
)@@G@@         JNS   A7,EXTP03 .   SHIFT SBW, -> CONSTANT SUBSCRIPT     @F@@@@BU
)@@G@@ . * COPY BOUNDS OF ALL STARRED BOUNDS IN ARGUMENT SUB-LIST *     @C@@@@BV
)@@G@@         LOAD  A6,W1+1,X6 .  ARGUMENT BOUNDS IN @C@@@@         STORE A6,BW
)@@G@@W1+1,X9 .  TEMPORARY'S BOUNDS @E@@@@         LOOP  A5,EXTP05 .   -> REPEBX
)@@G@@AT UNTIL ENOUGH STARRED @F@@@@ .                           BOUNDS HAVE BBY
)@@G@@EEN COPIED INTO TEMP    @E@@@@ . * SKIP NON-STARRED BOUNDS IN ARGUMENT TBZ
)@@G@@O FIND NEXT DV    @F@@@@EXTP09   LABEL .             MERGE FROM SCALER SCA
)@@G@@TRING PARAMETER   @F@@@@         ADD   X9,2,I .      BUMP POINTER TO NEXCB
)@@G@@T DOPE VECTOR     @H@@@@EXTP04   LABEL .             MERGE WHEN ARGUMENTCC
)@@G@@ IS ARRAY, PARM IS SCALER     @F@@@@         ADD   X6,2,I .      BUMP POCD
)@@G@@INTER NEXT SLOT IN ARGUMENT DV@F@@@@         JNS   A7,EXTP04 .   SHIFT, CE
)@@G@@-> LOOP WHILE CONSTANT SS     @C@@@@ . ** ALLOCATE STORAGE FOR CURRENT BCF
)@@G@@ASE ELEMENT @#@@@@EXTP10   LABEL .  @F@@@@         LINK  EXALL0 .      -CG
)@@G@@> FINISH ALLOCATION OF CURRENT ITEM @F@@@@EXTP06   LABEL .             CCH
)@@G@@OMPLETE SEARCH THROUGH STRUCTURE    @^@@@@         USING WORD,X4 .@F@@@@CI
)@@G@@         IF    A15,EQ,W1XU THEN,EXTP07 . -> ALLOCATION COMPLETE   @ @@@@CJ
)@@G@@         USING SDSECT,X4 .    @D@@@@         IF    SDBROT,ZERO THEN,EXTPCK
)@@G@@21 . -> NO BROTHER@F@@@@         LSDP  X4,SDBROT,X4 .          TEST BROTCL
)@@G@@HER FOR SON, ETC  @^@@@@         GOTO  EXTP11 . @#@@@@EXTP21   LABEL .  CM
)@@G@@@D@@@@         LSDP  X4,SDDAD,X4 . FOLLOW FATHER'S POINTER  @E@@@@      CN
)@@G@@   GOTO  EXTP06 .      -> TEST FATHER FOR BROTHER, ETC@B@@@@EXTP07   LABCO
)@@G@@EL .             FINISH UP    @E@@@@         LOAD  A1,W1XU,X7 .  RETURN CP
)@@G@@ADDRESS OF TEMPORARY DV @C@@@@         LMJ   X5,EXML .     RESTORE REGISCQ
)@@G@@TERS  @F@@@@         GOTO  2,X11 .       RETURN USING SAVED ADDRESS FROMCR
)@@G@@ AR   @I@@@@/ . --------------------------------------------------------CS
)@@G@@--------------------    @E@@@@ . *** EXECUTION CONTROL:  VARAIBLE DATA ACT
)@@G@@REA MANAGEMENT ***@I@@@@ . ---------------------------------------------CU
)@@G@@--------------------------------    @A@@@@ . OBTAIN NEW VARIABLE DATA ARCV
)@@G@@EA    @ @@@@         USING AREC,X10 .     @E@@@@EXGDVA*  LLOC .         CW
)@@G@@     ENTRY POINT FROM USER CODE     @H@@@@         LOAD  A1,AREPTR,X10 .CX
)@@G@@         END OF CURRENT VARIABLE DATA AREA (VDA)@F@@@@         LOAD  R1,CY
)@@G@@ARVDAP,X10 .         SAVE END OF PREVIOUS VDA   @C@@@@         STORE R1,CZ
)@@G@@W1,A1 .   IN NEXT FREE WORD   @H@@@@         STORE A1,ARVDAP,X10 .      DA
)@@G@@   VDA POINTER POINTS TO THAT POINTER     @E@@@@         ADD   A1,1,I . DB
)@@G@@NEW VDA STARTS JUST BEYOND POINTER  @G@@@@         STORE A1,AREPTR,X10 .DC
)@@G@@         END PTR POINTS TO FIRST FREE WORD@C@@@@         LJMP .         DD
)@@G@@     -> RETURN TO CALLER@H@@@@/ . --------------------------------------DE
)@@G@@------------------------------------@E@@@@ . CALLED BY CODE FOR SOURCE "DF
)@@G@@STOP" OR "EXIT" STATEMENT     @H@@@@ . ---------------------------------DG
)@@G@@------------------------------------------@#@@@@EXSTOP*  LABEL .  @F@@@@DH
)@@G@@         STORE   R11,ARSTMT .      SET STATEMENT NUMBER FOR PMD   @^@@@@DI
)@@G@@ . 'PROGRAM IS STOPPED.'@G@@@@   ONUNIT  EREXSTOP,ACCDFN,0,I  PLEXND,PLEDJ
)@@G@@XND,PLEXND  DEXWK1,0  DEXMAX,0@C@@@@ . ** ROUTINE TO HANDLE IMPROPER STRDK
)@@G@@ING LENGTHS @B@@@@EXTMSL   LOCAL .             ENTRY POINT  @ @@@@      DL
)@@G@@   ONER EREXTMSL,2 .    @G@@@@ . 'STRING LENGTH ', NUMA5, ' OF ',SDX4, 'DM
)@@G@@ IS IMPROPER.  80 IS USED.'   @D@@@@         LOAD  A5,80,I .     CORRECTDN
)@@G@@ION STRING LENGTH @C@@@@         JMP .               -> RETURN TO CALLERDO
)@@G@@@I@@@@/. ---------------------------------------------------------------DP
)@@G@@--------------    @C@@@@ . ** PREPARE MULTIPLE SUBSCRIPT LIST ENTRIES **DQ
)@@G@@@I@@@@ . ---------------------------------------------------------------DR
)@@G@@--------------    @F@@@@ . ADDS A LIST OF TALLY CELL INDICIES TO A LIST DS
)@@G@@OF LOWER BOUNDS   @C@@@@ . TO PRODUCE A LIST OF FULLWORD SUBSCRIPTS     DT
)@@G@@@]@@@@ . INPUT:   @A@@@@ .       A1 = A(TALLY CELL INDEX)   @A@@@@ .    DU
)@@G@@   A2 = A(NEXT LOWER BOUND)   @B@@@@ .       A3 = A(NEXT SUBSCRIPT LIST DV
)@@G@@SLOT) @E@@@@ .       R1 = LOOP COUNT = NUMBER OF CONSECUTIVE STARS - 1  DW
)@@G@@@A@@@@ . DESTROYS:  A1, A2, A3, AND R1    @B@@@@EXPMSL*  LLOC .         DX
)@@G@@     ENTRY POINT  @D@@@@         LOADXI A1,1,I .     TALLY CELL INCREMENDY
)@@G@@TOR   @D@@@@         LOADXI A2,2,I .     DOPE VECTOR INCREMENTOR  @E@@@@DZ
)@@G@@         LOADXI A3,1,I .     SUBSCRIPT LIST INCREMENTOR     @#@@@@EXPMS1EA
)@@G@@   LABEL .  @E@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1XH2,*A1 .          TALLY CELL OFFSEB
)@@G@@ET    @H@@@@         ADD   A4,W1XH2,*A2 .          TRUE SUBSCRIPT VALUE EC
)@@G@@FROM LOWER BOUND  @D@@@@         STORE A4,W1,*A3 .   PUT IN SUBSCRIPT LIED
)@@G@@ST    @D@@@@         LOOP  R1,EXPMS1 .   -> MORE STAR SUBSCRIPTS  @D@@@@EE
)@@G@@         LJMP .              -> RETURN TO USER CODE   @I@@@@ . ---------EF
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------------    EG
)@@G@@@D@@@@ . ** USER CODE CORRECTION FOR NEGATIVE EXTENT - 1    @I@@@@ . ---EH
)@@G@@------------------------------------------------------------------------EI
)@@G@@--    @H@@@@EXJGDE*  LOCAL .             EXTENT - 1 WAS COMPUTED NEGATIVEJ
)@@G@@E IN USER CODE    @E@@@@         SUB   X11,2,I .     GET ADDRESS OF JGD EK
)@@G@@BEFORE LINK @G@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1Q2,X11 . GET REGISTER ADDRESS CONTEL
)@@G@@AINING EXTENT - 1 @E@@@@         SRB   A3,4 .        RIGHT JUSTIFY REGISEM
)@@G@@TER ADDRESS @C@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1,A3 .    IMPROPER EXTENT - 1@D@@@@EN
)@@G@@         ADD   A4,1,I .      COMPUTE IMPROPER EXTENT  @F@@@@         ONUEO
)@@G@@NIT  EREXJGDE,ACCDSU,2  R,I,R  DEXWK1,4  DEXMAX,4     @C@@@@.        USEEP
)@@G@@ LOWER BOUND : LOWERBOUND + 10 .    @H@@@@ . 'UPPER BOUND', NUMA4, 'WAS EQ
)@@G@@LESS THAN LOWER BOUND OF 1.  (1:10) IS USED.'   @D@@@@         LOAD  A4,ER
)@@G@@9,I .      SET REPAIRED EXTENT - 1  @C@@@@         STORE A4,W1,A3 .    RES
)@@G@@EPLACE IN REGISTER@B@@@@         JMP . -> RETURN TO USER CODE     @I@@@@ET
)@@G@@/. ---------------------------------------------------------------------EU
)@@G@@--------    @B@@@@ . ** FIXED BINARY HALFWORD OVERFLOW **   @I@@@@ . ---EV
)@@G@@------------------------------------------------------------------------EW
)@@G@@--    @D@@@@ . CALLED BY USER CODE WHEN VALUE IS TOO LARGE TO     @C@@@@EX
)@@G@@ . FITTED INTO A FIXED BINARY HALFWORD (17,0).  @F@@@@ . A CORRECTION ISEY
)@@G@@ MADE TO THE REGISTER CONTAINING THE OPERAND    @C@@@@EXHWOV*  LOCAL .  EZ
)@@G@@           SAVE RETURN ADDRESS@G@@@@         SUB   X11,2,I .     GET REGFA
)@@G@@ISTER NUMBER FROM TG,U A,0400000    @E@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1Q2,X11 . RFB
)@@G@@EGISTER  NUMBER WITH SHIFT    @E@@@@         SRB   A3,4 .        RIGHT JFC
)@@G@@USTIFY REGISTER NUMBER  @D@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1+A0,A3 . FETCH INCORREFD
)@@G@@CT VALUE    @F@@@@         ONUNIT  EREXHWOV,ACCDSI,2  R,I,JMP  DEXWK1,4 FE
)@@G@@ DEXMAX,4   @E@@@@ . 'LENGTH OR BOUND', NUMA4, ' IS TOO LARGE.  10 IS USFF
)@@G@@ED.'  @D@@@@         LOAD  A4,10,I .     USE CORRECTION OF 10     @E@@@@FG
)@@G@@         STORE A4,W1+A0,A3 . SET CORRECTION INTO REGISTER   @C@@@@      FH
)@@G@@   JMP . -> RETURN TO CALLER IN USER CODE @D@@@@EXMST*   LLOC .         FI
)@@G@@     RETURN ADDRESS IN X5     @F@@@@         STORE R11,ARSTMT,X10 .     FJ
)@@G@@    SAVE STATEMENT NUMBER     @G@@@@         STORE X11,ARSV11,X10 .     FK
)@@G@@   SAVE MODIFIERS OF BASE REGISTERS @ @@@@         STORE X7,ARSVX7,X10 .FL
)@@G@@@ @@@@         STORE X8,ARSVX8,X10 .@ @@@@         STORE X9,ARSVX9,X10 .FM
)@@G@@@F@@@@         STORED A5,ARSVA5,X10 .        SAVE 'A' REGISTER PAIRS    FN
)@@G@@@A@@@@         STORED A7,ARSVA7,X10 .     @A@@@@         STORED A9,ARSVAFO
)@@G@@9,X10 .     @A@@@@         STORED A11,ARSA11,X10 .    @A@@@@         STOFP
)@@G@@RED A13,ARSA13,X10 .    @A@@@@         STORED A15,ARSA15,X10 .    @E@@@@FQ
)@@G@@         STORE X1,ARSAX1,X10 .         SAVE I/O REGISTERS   @ @@@@      FR
)@@G@@   STORE X2,ARSAX2,X10 .@ @@@@         STORE X3,ARSAX3,X10 .@F@@@@      FS
)@@G@@   STORE   X6,ARSVX6,X10 .    SAVE MANAGED 'X' REGISTERS    @A@@@@      FT
)@@G@@   STORE   X4,ARSVX4,X10 .    @C@@@@         GOTO  0,X5 .        ->RETURFU
)@@G@@N TO CALLER @D@@@@EXML*    LLOC .              RETURN ADDRESS IN X5     FV
)@@G@@@F@@@@         LOAD  R11,ARSTMT,X10 .         RESTORE STATEMENT NUMBER  FW
)@@G@@@H@@@@         LOADXM X11,ARSV11,X10 .       RESTORE MODIFIERS OF BASE RFX
)@@G@@EGISTERS    @A@@@@         LOADXM X7,ARSVX7,X10 .     @A@@@@         LOAFY
)@@G@@DXM X8,ARSVX8,X10 .     @A@@@@         LOADXM X9,ARSVX9,X10 .     @F@@@@FZ

)@@G@@--------------------------------    @A@@@@ . *** CROSS SECTION COMPUTER GR
)@@G@@***   @ @@@@ . CALLED BY COMPILIED CODE   @C@@@@ . A1  = ADDRESS OF LISTGS
)@@G@@ OF FULLWORD SUBSCRIPTS @E@@@@ . A2  = ADDRESS OF DOPE VECTOR FROM WHICHGT
)@@G@@ CROSS SECTION    @A@@@@ .            IS TO BE COMPUTED     @F@@@@ . X11GU
)@@G@@ --->             W          (FLAG BITS) SELECTOR BITS WORD @D@@@@ .    GV

)@@G@@RD, BIT N IS ON IF SUBSCRIPT N + 1  @B@@@@ .       IN SUPPLIED LIST IS NGZ

)@@G@@ MAY BE USED TO REFERENCE     @F@@@@ . THE DESIGNATED CROSS-SECTION IN THB

)@@G@@@D@@@@EXCRSC*  LOCAL .             ENTRY FROM COMPILED CODE @D@@@@      HP

)@@G@@         LOADXM A2,AREPTR,X10 .        FIRST AVAILABLE WORD ON STACK    HY
)@@G@@@D@@@@         STORE A2,DEXWK2 .   SAVE TO LOAD A1 AT END   @G@@@@EXCRS1HZ
)@@G@@   LABEL .             FOLLOW POINTERS THROUGH SD'S OF STRUCTURE  @C@@@@IA
)@@G@@         USING SDSECT,A1 .   TO BASIC ELEMENTS  @G@@@@         IF    SDSIB
)@@G@@TRU,OFF,SDCLS4 THEN,EXCRS2 . -> BASE ELEMENT FOUND    @D@@@@         LOAIC
)@@G@@D  A1,SDSON,A1 . FOLLOW SD POINTER TO SON @C@@@@         GOTO  EXCRS1 . ID
)@@G@@     ->CHECK THE SON    @G@@@@EXCRS2   LABEL .             CONSTRUCT DOPIE
)@@G@@E VECTOR FOR CROSS SECTION    @C@@@@ .                           OF THISIF
)@@G@@ BASE ARRAY @A@@@@         LOAD  A6,DEXWK3 .   SBW    @C@@@@         LOAIG
)@@G@@D  X3,R1 .       GET LOOP COUNT     @E@@@@         LOAD  X5,A2 .       SIH
)@@G@@AVE START OF DOPE VECTOR (NEW)@E@@@@         LOAD  A5,W1,X2 .    SAVE ORII
)@@G@@IGINAL VIRTUAL ORIGIN   @D@@@@         LOAD  A3,W1+1,*X2 . TRANSFER STRIIJ
)@@G@@NG LENGTHS  @C@@@@         STORE A3,W1+1,*A2 . TO NEW DOPE VECTOR @#@@@@IK
)@@G@@EXCRS3   LABEL .  @H@@@@         JNS   A6,EXCRS4 .   -> RIGHTMOST SBW BIIL
)@@G@@T ON, SUBSCRIPT IS NON-STAR   @F@@@@ . MULTIPLIER AND BOUNDS OF STARRED IM
)@@G@@SUBSCRIPT BECOME MULTIPLIER   @B@@@@ . AND BOUNDS OF CROSS SECTION DOPE IN
)@@G@@VECTOR@G@@@@         LOADD A3,W1,*X2 .   COPY MULTIPLIER, EXTENT-1, AND IO
)@@G@@LOWER BOUND @F@@@@         STORED A3,W1,*A2 .  MOVING POINTER TO NEXT SLIP
)@@G@@OT IN NEW DV@G@@@@         LOADXM  X1,W1U+1,X1 .     BUMP TO NEXT SLOT IIQ
)@@G@@N SUBSCRIPT LIST  @E@@@@EXCRS8   LABEL .                   TRY FOR MORE IR
)@@G@@STORAGE     @D@@@@         LOAD    A4,W1U,A2 .       SEE IF IT WILL FIT IS
)@@G@@@E@@@@         IF    A4,LT,ADPCND THEN,EXCRS5 . ->WILL IT FIT?    @E@@@@IT
)@@G@@         LINK    WROVFL .          TRY TO GET MORE STORAGE  @E@@@@      IU
)@@G@@   GOTO  EXCRS8 .      -> STILL WITHIN STACK BOUNDS   @#@@@@EXCRS4   LABIV
)@@G@@EL .  @D@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1,*X1 .   PICK UP SUBSCRIPT VALUE  @E@@@@IW
)@@G@@         LOAD  A3,W1+1,X2 .  GET EXTENT-1 AND LOWER BOUND   @H@@@@      IX
)@@G@@   TLE,XU A4,0,*A3 .TEST SUBSCRIPT AGAINST LOWER BOUND AND COMPUTE UPPERIY
)@@G@@@D@@@@         GOTO  EXCRCL .      -> SUBSCRIPT TOO LOW     @^@@@@      IZ
)@@G@@   USING WORD,A3 .@F@@@@         IF    A4,GE,W1XU+1 THEN,EXCRCU . -> SUBJA
)@@G@@SCRIPT TOO HIGH   @E@@@@EXCRSE   LABEL .             MERGE AFTER ERROR CJB
)@@G@@ORRECTION   @H@@@@         MPYS  A4,W1,*X2 .   SUBSCRIPT*MULTIPLIER, ADVJC
)@@G@@ANCE OLD DV POINTER     @E@@@@         ADD   A5,A4 .       ACCUMULATE WIJD
)@@G@@TH VIRTUAL ORIGIN @#@@@@EXCRS5   LABEL .  @E@@@@         LOOP  X3,EXCRS3JE
)@@G@@ .   -> REPEAT FOR EACH SUBSCRIPT   @D@@@@         STORE A5,W1,*X5 .   IJF
)@@G@@NSERT NEW VIRTUAL ORIGIN@F@@@@         IF    A2,NE,X5 THEN,EXCRS6 . -> CJG
)@@G@@ROSS SECTION IS AN ARRAY@ @@@@         USING SDSECT,A1 .    @E@@@@      JH
)@@G@@   IF    SDARST,ON,SDCLS1 THEN,EXCRS6 . -> STRING     @F@@@@         SUBJI
)@@G@@   A2,1,I .      SCALER, NON-STRING USES ONLY 1 WORD  @I@@@@EXCRS6   LABJJ
)@@G@@EL .             CONTINUE SEARCHING THROUNG STRUCTURE FOR BASE ELEME    JK
)@@G@@@H@@@@         IF    A1,EQ,DEXWK1 THEN,EXCRS7 . -> WE'RE BACK TO ORIGINAJL
)@@G@@L SD, DONE  @F@@@@         IF    SDBROT,NZERO THEN,EXCRS9 . -> FOLLOW SDJM
)@@G@@ TO BROTHER @E@@@@         LOAD  A1,SDDAD,A1 . -> TEST FATHER FOR BROTHEJN
)@@G@@R, ETC@^@@@@         GOTO  EXCRS6 . @#@@@@EXCRS9   LABEL .  @G@@@@      JO
)@@G@@   LOAD  A1,SDBROT,A1 .          FOLLOW SD POINTER TO BROTHER     @^@@@@JP
)@@G@@         GOTO  EXCRS1 . @#@@@@EXCRS7   LABEL .  @^@@@@         LOADXI A2JQ
)@@G@@,0,I .@F@@@@         TNG,XH2 A2,DEXMAX-(IN 63,H2,1,0) . TEST FOR NEW STAJR
)@@G@@CK MAX@D@@@@         STORE A2,DEXMAX .   SET NEW MAX STACK HEIGHT @E@@@@JS
)@@G@@         STORE A2,AREPTR .   NEW TOP OF ACTIVATION RECORD   @D@@@@      JT
)@@G@@   LOAD  A1,DEXWK2+FH2 .         POINT TO NEW DV@^@@@@         LINK  EXUJU
)@@G@@NSV . @F@@@@         JMP   2 .           -> RETURN SKIPPING ARGUMENT LISJV
)@@G@@T     @#@@@@EXCRCL   LABEL .  @C@@@@         LOAD  A4,W1XU,X2 .  USE LOWJW
)@@G@@ER BOUND    @#@@@@EXCRCE   LABEL .  @D@@@@         LOAD    X4,X1 .      JX
)@@G@@     HOLD FOR LATER     @E@@@@         LOAD    X1,R1 .           GET NUMJY
)@@G@@BER OF DIMS-1     @E@@@@         SUB     X1,W1U,X3 .       SUB OFF NUMBEJZ
)@@G@@R LEFT-1    @D@@@@         ADD     X1,1,I .          MAKE ONE ORIGIN    KA
)@@G@@@E@@@@         ONUNIT  EREXSB,ACCDSU,2  R,I,R  DEXWK1,4  DEXMAX,4 @D@@@@KB
)@@G@@         LOAD    X1,X4 .           RECLAIM REGISTER   @E@@@@ . 'SUBSCRIPKC
)@@G@@T ', X1, ' OF ', SDA1, ' IS OUT OF BOUNDS.'     @C@@@@         GOTO  EXCKD
)@@G@@RSE .      -> RETURN TO CALLER@#@@@@EXCRCU   LABEL .  @C@@@@         LOAKE
)@@G@@D  A4,W1XU,A3 .  USE UPPER BOUND    @^@@@@         GOTO  EXCRCE . @E@@@@KF
)@@G@@         END . EXECUTION DRIVER AND ARRAY SERVICE ROUTINES  ___         KG
